      display: block !important; } }
  @media screen and (orientation: portrait) {

    .hide-for-portrait {
      display: none !important; } }

           */ }

  opacity: 0;
  transition: opacity 400ms ease; }

  max-height: 0; }

  transform-style: preserve-3d; }
